       <script>(function() {var fragmentElement = document.querySelector('#fragment-1982327-vzef'); var configuration = {"visibility":"all viewports"};$(document).ready(function () {



    const $parent = $('#tzoker-jackpot-bar');

    const $banner = $parent.find('.placeholder');

    const templates = {

        fallback: Handlebars.compile($('#jackpot-banner-fallback').html()),

        jackpot: Handlebars.compile($('#jackpot-banner-jackpot').html()),

        freeze: Handlebars.compile($('#jackpot-banner-freeze').html()),

        single: Handlebars.compile($('#jackpot-banner-single').html()),

        multiple: Handlebars.compile($('#jackpot-banner-multiple').html())

    };



    try {



        const freeze = contextContributor.tzoker.freeze;

        const active = contextContributor.tzoker.results.active;

        const last = contextContributor.tzoker.results.last;



        const lang = $('html')[0].lang === 'el-GR' ? 'el' : 'en';

        const ticketSubmission = moment(active.drawTime - active.drawBreak).locale(lang).format('dddd HH:mm');



        const ticketHTML = Handlebars.compile($('#submission-text').html());

        $('#countdown-text-desktop').empty().append(ticketHTML({ticketSubmission}));



        if (freeze) {

            /** freeze */

            $banner.empty().append(templates.freeze({}));

        } else if (last.prizeCategories[0].winners == 0 && active.prizeCategories[0].minimumDistributed) {

            /** jackpot */

            $banner.empty().append(templates.jackpot({

                amount: '€' + Math.round(active.prizeCategories[0].minimumDistributed).toLocaleString('el-GR')

            }));

        } else if (last.prizeCategories[0].winners == 1) {

            /** single winner */

            $banner.empty().append(templates.single({

                amount: '€' + Math.round(last.prizeCategories[0].divident).toLocaleString('el-GR')

            }));

        } else if (last.prizeCategories[0].winners > 1) {

            /** multiple winners */

            $banner.empty().append(templates.multiple({

                winners: last.prizeCategories[0].winners,

                amount: '€' + Math.ceil(last.prizeCategories[0].jackpot + last.prizeCategories[0].distributed).toLocaleString("el-GR")

            }));

        } else {

            throw new Error('Tzoker automated banner could not determine the appropriate banner and instead rendered the fallback');

        }



    } catch (err) {

        /** fallback */

        $banner.empty().append(templates.fallback({}));

        console.warn(err);

    }



});;}());</script> 

      </section>

  <script type="text/javascript">



    var RENDER_TIME = Date.now();

    var $tzokerDays, $tzokerHours, $tzokerMins, $tzokerSecs;

    var $protoDays, $protoHours, $protoMins, $protoSecs;

    var $lottoDays, $lottoHours, $lottoMins, $lottoSecs;

    var $kinoDrawID, $kinoDrawTime, $kinoHours, $kinoMins, $kinoSecs;

    var $tzokerDrawContent, $protoDrawContent, $kinoDrawContent;

    var server = Object.assign(window.server || {

        ticking: false,

        games: {

            tzoker: {

                draws: {

                    next: {

                        days: "00",

                        hours: "00",

                        minutes: "00",

                        seconds: "00"

                    }

                }

            },

            proto: {

                draws: {

                    next: {

                        days: "00",

                        hours: "00",

                        minutes: "00",

                        seconds: "00"

                    }

                }

            },

            lotto: {

                draws: {

                    next: {

                        days: "00",

                        hours: "00",

                        minutes: "00",

                        seconds: "00"

                    }

                }

            },

            kino: {

                draws: {

                    next: {

                        drawID: "0001",

                        drawTime: "00:00",

                        hours: "00",

                        minutes: "00",

                        seconds: "00"

                    }

                }

            }

        }

    }, {

        timestamp: 1675702060527

    })



    var updateTzokerSelectors = function () {

        $tzokerDrawContent = $('.draw-content[data-game="tzoker"]');

        $tzokerDays = $('.metric-days[data-game="tzoker"]');

        $tzokerHours = $('.metric-hours[data-game="tzoker"]');

        $tzokerMins = $('.metric-mins[data-game="tzoker"]');

        $tzokerSecs = $('.metric-secs[data-game="tzoker"]');

    }



    var updateProtoSelectors = function () {

        $protoDrawContent = $('.draw-content[data-game="proto"]');

        $protoDays = $('.metric-days[data-game="proto"]');

        $protoHours = $('.metric-hours[data-game="proto"]');

        $protoMins = $('.metric-mins[data-game="proto"]');

        $protoSecs = $('.metric-secs[data-game="proto"]');

    }



    var updateLottoSelectors = function () {

        $lottoDrawContent = $('.draw-content[data-game="lotto"]');

        $lottoDays = $('.metric-days[data-game="lotto"]');

        $lottoHours = $('.metric-hours[data-game="lotto"]');

        $lottoMins = $('.metric-mins[data-game="lotto"]');

        $lottoSecs = $('.metric-secs[data-game="lotto"]');

    }



    var updateKinoSelectors = function () {

        $kinoDrawContent = $('.draw-content[data-game="kino"]');

        $kinoDrawID = $('.draw-id[data-game="kino"]');

        $kinoDrawTime = $('.draw-time[data-game="kino"]');

        $kinoHours = $('.metric-hours[data-game="kino"]');

        $kinoMins = $('.metric-mins[data-game="kino"]');

        $kinoSecs = $('.metric-secs[data-game="kino"]');

    }



    var fetchKinoLastResultAndActive = function (callback) {



        $.get(`https://api.opap.gr/draws/v3.0/1100/last-result-and-active`).done(function (results) {



            contextContributor.kino.results = results;



            window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent("KinoContextContributor"));



            if (callback instanceof Function) {

                callback();

            }



        });



    }



    var tzokerTickerPerSec = function () {



        try {



            if (!contextContributor.tzoker.freeze && !$(document.body).hasClass("tzoker-draw")) {



                if (contextContributor.tzoker.results) {



                    var results = contextContributor.tzoker.results;

                    var original_diff = Math.round((results.active.drawTime - window.server.timestamp) / 1000);

                    var diff = original_diff;



                    var days = 0;

                    var hours = 0;

                    var minutes = 0;



                    while (diff >= 86400) {

                        diff -= 86400;

                        days++;

                    }



                    while (diff >= 3600) {

                        diff -= 3600;

                        hours++;

                    }



                    while (diff >= 60) {

                        diff -= 60;

                        minutes++;

                    }



                    server.games.tzoker.draws.next = {

                        days: ("00" + days).substr(-2, 2),

                        hours: ("00" + hours).substr(-2, 2),

                        minutes: ("00" + minutes).substr(-2, 2),

                        seconds: ("00" + diff).substr(-2, 2)

                    };



                }



            } else {

                server.games.tzoker.draws.next.days = "00";

                server.games.tzoker.draws.next.hours = "00";

                server.games.tzoker.draws.next.minutes = "00";

                server.games.tzoker.draws.next.seconds = "00";

            }



            $tzokerDays.text(server.games.tzoker.draws.next.days);

            $tzokerHours.text(server.games.tzoker.draws.next.hours);

            $tzokerMins.text(server.games.tzoker.draws.next.minutes);

            $tzokerSecs.text(server.games.tzoker.draws.next.seconds);



            if ((contextContributor.tzoker.freeze || original_diff <= 0) && !$(document.body).hasClass("tzoker-draw")) {



                $(document.body).addClass("tzoker-draw");



                $tzokerDrawContent.each(function () {



                    var $this = $(this);



                    $this.addClass($this.data("class-on-draw"));



                })



                server.games.tzoker.draws.next.days = "00";

                server.games.tzoker.draws.next.hours = "00";

                server.games.tzoker.draws.next.minutes = "00";

                server.games.tzoker.draws.next.seconds = "00";



            }



            $tzokerDays.text(server.games.tzoker.draws.next.days);

            $tzokerHours.text(server.games.tzoker.draws.next.hours);

            $tzokerMins.text(server.games.tzoker.draws.next.minutes);

            $tzokerSecs.text(server.games.tzoker.draws.next.seconds);



        } catch (err) {

            console.error(err);

        }



    }



    var protoTickerPerSec = function () {



        try {



            if (contextContributor.proto.results) {



                var results = contextContributor.proto.results;

                var original_diff = Math.round((results.active.drawTime - window.server.timestamp) / 1000);

                var diff = original_diff;



                var days = 0;

                var hours = 0;

                var minutes = 0;



                while (diff >= 86400) {

                    diff -= 86400;

                    days++;

                }



                while (diff >= 3600) {

                    diff -= 3600;

                    hours++;

                }



                while (diff >= 60) {

                    diff -= 60;

                    minutes++;

                }



                server.games.proto.draws.next = {

                    days: ("00" + days).substr(-2, 2),

                    hours: ("00" + hours).substr(-2, 2),

                    minutes: ("00" + minutes).substr(-2, 2),

                    seconds: ("00" + diff).substr(-2, 2)

                };



            }



            if ((contextContributor.proto.freeze || original_diff <= 0) && !$(document.body).hasClass("proto-draw")) {



                $(document.body).addClass("proto-draw");



                $protoDrawContent.each(function () {



                    var $this = $(this);



                    $this.addClass($this.data("class-on-draw"));



                })



                server.games.proto.draws.next.days = "00";

                server.games.proto.draws.next.hours = "00";

                server.games.proto.draws.next.minutes = "00";

                server.games.proto.draws.next.seconds = "00";



            }



            $protoDays.text(server.games.proto.draws.next.days);

            $protoHours.text(server.games.proto.draws.next.hours);

            $protoMins.text(server.games.proto.draws.next.minutes);

            $protoSecs.text(server.games.proto.draws.next.seconds);



        } catch (err) {

            console.error(err);

        }



    }



    var lottoTickerPerSec = function () {



        try {



            if (contextContributor.lotto.results) {



                var results = contextContributor.lotto.results;

                var original_diff = Math.round((results.active.drawTime - window.server.timestamp) / 1000);

                var diff = original_diff;



                var days = 0;

                var hours = 0;

                var minutes = 0;



                while (diff >= 86400) {

                    diff -= 86400;

                    days++;

                }



                while (diff >= 3600) {

                    diff -= 3600;

                    hours++;

                }



                while (diff >= 60) {

                    diff -= 60;

                    minutes++;

                }



                server.games.lotto.draws.next = {

                    days: ("00" + days).substr(-2, 2),

                    hours: ("00" + hours).substr(-2, 2),

                    minutes: ("00" + minutes).substr(-2, 2),

                    seconds: ("00" + diff).substr(-2, 2)

                };



            }



            if ((contextContributor.lotto.freeze || original_diff <= 0) && !$(document.body).hasClass("lotto-draw")) {



                $(document.body).addClass("lotto-draw");



                $lottoDrawContent.each(function () {



                    var $this = $(this);



                    $this.addClass($this.data("class-on-draw"));



                })



                server.games.lotto.draws.next.days = "00";

                server.games.lotto.draws.next.hours = "00";

                server.games.lotto.draws.next.minutes = "00";

                server.games.lotto.draws.next.seconds = "00";



            }



            $lottoDays.text(server.games.lotto.draws.next.days);

            $lottoHours.text(server.games.lotto.draws.next.hours);

            $lottoMins.text(server.games.lotto.draws.next.minutes);

            $lottoSecs.text(server.games.lotto.draws.next.seconds);



        } catch (err) {

            console.error(err);

        }



    }



    var kinoTickerPerSec = function () {



        try {



            if (contextContributor.kino.results) {



                var results = contextContributor.kino.results;

                var original_diff = Math.round((results.active.drawTime - window.server.timestamp) / 1000);

                var diff = original_diff;



                if (diff <= 0) {

                    diff += 300;

                }



                var hours = 0;

                var minutes = 0;



                while (diff >= 3600) {

                    diff -= 3600;

                    hours++;

                }



                while (diff >= 60) {

                    diff -= 60;

                    minutes++;

                }



                server.games.kino.draws.next = {

                    drawID: results.active.drawId,

                    drawTime: results.active.drawTime,

                    hours: hours >= 0 ? ("00" + hours).substr(-2, 2) : "00",

                    minutes: minutes >= 0 ? ("00" + minutes).substr(-2, 2) : "00",

                    seconds: diff >= 0 ? ("00" + diff).substr(-2, 2) : "00"

                };



                if (server.games.kino.draws.next.hours > 0) {

                    $('.kino-atb-hours').removeClass('d-none');

                }



                if (original_diff <= 20 && original_diff >= 0) {

                    $('.metric-secs[data-game="kino"]').parent().addClass('red-metric');

                } else {

                    $('.metric-secs[data-game="kino"]').parent().removeClass('red-metric');

                }



                $kinoDrawID.text(server.games.kino.draws.next.drawID);

                $kinoDrawTime.text(moment(server.games.kino.draws.next.drawTime, "x").format("HH:mm"));

                $kinoHours.text(server.games.kino.draws.next.hours);

                $kinoMins.text(server.games.kino.draws.next.minutes);

                $kinoSecs.text(server.games.kino.draws.next.seconds);



            }



            if (!contextContributor.kino.freeze && (original_diff <= 0 && original_diff <= (contextContributor.kino.drawOffset * -1))) {



                contextContributor.kino.freeze = true;



                window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent("KinoRerender", {

                    detail: {

                        done: updateKinoSelectors,

                        next: server.games.kino.draws.next

                    }

                }));



                $(document.body).addClass("kino-draw");



                $kinoDrawContent.each(function () {



                    var $this = $(this);



                    $this.addClass($this.data("class-on-draw"));



                });



            } else if (contextContributor.kino.freeze && original_diff < (contextContributor.kino.drawOffset * -1)) {



                fetchKinoLastResultAndActive(function () {



                    contextContributor.kino.freeze = false;



                    window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent("KinoRerender", {

                        detail: {

                            done: updateKinoSelectors,

                            next: server.games.kino.draws.next

                        }

                    }));



                    $(document.body).removeClass("kino-draw");



                    $kinoDrawContent.each(function () {



                        var $this = $(this);



                        $this.removeClass($this.data("class-on-draw"));



                    });



                });

            }



        } catch (err) {

            console.error(err);

        }



    }



    var perSecloop = function () {



        tzokerTickerPerSec();

        protoTickerPerSec();

        lottoTickerPerSec();

        kinoTickerPerSec();



        window.server.timestamp += 1000;



        setTimeout(perSecloop, 1000);



    }



    var init = function () {



        $tzokerDrawContent = $('.draw-content[data-game="tzoker"]');

        $tzokerDays = $('.metric-days[data-game="tzoker"]');

        $tzokerHours = $('.metric-hours[data-game="tzoker"]');

        $tzokerMins = $('.metric-mins[data-game="tzoker"]');

        $tzokerSecs = $('.metric-secs[data-game="tzoker"]');



        $protoDrawContent = $('.draw-content[data-game="proto"]');

        $protoDays = $('.metric-days[data-game="proto"]');

        $protoHours = $('.metric-hours[data-game="proto"]');

        $protoMins = $('.metric-mins[data-game="proto"]');

        $protoSecs = $('.metric-secs[data-game="proto"]');



        $lottoDrawContent = $('.draw-content[data-game="lotto"]');

        $lottoDays = $('.metric-days[data-game="lotto"]');

        $lottoHours = $('.metric-hours[data-game="lotto"]');

        $lottoMins = $('.metric-mins[data-game="lotto"]');

        $lottoSecs = $('.metric-secs[data-game="lotto"]');



        $kinoDrawContent = $('.draw-content[data-game="kino"]');

        $kinoDrawID = $('.draw-id[data-game="kino"]');

        $kinoDrawTime = $('.draw-time[data-game="kino"]');

        $kinoHours = $('.metric-hours[data-game="kino"]');

        $kinoMins = $('.metric-mins[data-game="kino"]');

        $kinoSecs = $('.metric-secs[data-game="kino"]');



        window.server.timestamp = window.server.timestamp + (Date.now() - RENDER_TIME);



        if (!window.server.ticking) {

            window.server.ticking = true;

            perSecloop();

        }



    }



    fetchKinoLastResultAndActive();



    $(document).ready(init);

    document.addEventListener("visibilitychange", () => {

        if (document.visibilityState === "visible") window.server.timestamp = Date.now();

    });



</script>

  <script type="text/javascript">

// <![CDATA[



	

		Liferay.Portlet.register('com_liferay_journal_content_web_portlet_JournalContentPortlet_INSTANCE_userwidgetcontainertzoker');

	



	Liferay.Portlet.onLoad(

(function() {var $ = AUI.$;var _ = AUI._;

	var onVote = function(event) {

		if (window.Analytics) {

			Analytics.send('VOTE', 'Ratings', {

				className: event.className,

				classPK: event.classPK,

				ratingType: event.ratingType,

				score: event.score

			});

		}

	};



	var onDestroyPortlet = function() {

		Liferay.detach('ratings:vote', onVote);

		Liferay.detach('destroyPortlet', onDestroyPortlet);

	};



	Liferay.on('ratings:vote', onVote);

	Liferay.on('destroyPortlet', onDestroyPortlet);

})();(function() {var $ = AUI.$;var _ = AUI._;

	var pathnameRegexp = /\/documents\/(\d+)\/(\d+)\/(.+?)\/([^&]+)/;



	function handleDownloadClick(event) {

		if (event.target.nodeName.toLowerCase() === 'a' && window.Analytics) {

			var anchor = event.target;

			var match = pathnameRegexp.exec(anchor.pathname);



			var fileEntryId =

				anchor.dataset.analyticsFileEntryId ||

				(anchor.parentElement &&

					anchor.parentElement.dataset.analyticsFileEntryId);



			if (fileEntryId && match) {

				var getParameterValue = function(parameterName) {

					var result = null;



					anchor.search

						.substr(1)

						.split('&')

						.forEach(function(item) {

							var tmp = item.split('=');



							if (tmp[0] === parameterName) {

								result = decodeURIComponent(tmp[1]);

							}

						});



					return result;

				};



				Analytics.send('documentDownloaded', 'Document', {

					groupId: match[1],

					fileEntryId: fileEntryId,

					preview: !!window._com_liferay_document_library_analytics_isViewFileEntry,

					title: decodeURIComponent(match[3].replace(/\+/gi, ' ')),

					version: getParameterValue('version')

				});

			}

		}

	}



	var onDestroyPortlet = function() {

		document.body.removeEventListener('click', handleDownloadClick);

	};



	Liferay.once('destroyPortlet', onDestroyPortlet);



	var onPortletReady = function() {

		document.body.addEventListener('click', handleDownloadClick);

	};



	Liferay.once('portletReady', onPortletReady);

})();(function() {var $ = AUI.$;var _ = AUI._;

	var onShare = function(data) {

		if (window.Analytics) {

			Analytics.send('shared', 'SocialBookmarks', {

				className: data.className,

				classPK: data.classPK,

				type: data.type,

				url: data.url

			});

		}

	};



	var onDestroyPortlet = function() {

		Liferay.detach('socialBookmarks:share', onShare);

		Liferay.detach('destroyPortlet', onDestroyPortlet);

	};



	Liferay.on('socialBookmarks:share', onShare);

	Liferay.on('destroyPortlet', onDestroyPortlet);

		}

	};



	Liferay.on('messagePosted', onMessagePosted);

        var createSalesforceScript = function () {

            var s = document.createElement('script');

            s.setAttribute('src', 'https://opap.my.salesforce.com/embeddedservice/5.0/esw.min.js');

            s.setAttribute('id', 'salesforceScript');

            s.onload = function () {

                initESW(null);

            };

            document.body.appendChild(s);

        };



        var removeSalesforceScript = function () {

            $('#salesforceScript').remove();

        };



        var salesforceLogicFlow = function () {

            if (!window.embedded_svc) {

                removeSalesforceScript();

                createSalesforceScript();

            } else {

                initESW('https://service.force.com');

            }

        }



        salesforceLogicFlow();



        var launchChat = function (evt) {

            evt.preventDefault();



            $('.helpButtonEnabled').trigger('click');

        }

                if (evt.type === 'salesforceUserLoginEvent') {

                    if (!window.embedded_svc.settings.prepopulatedPrechatFields.PlayerID__c) {

                        console.debug('User login detected - reloading salesforce script');

                        salesforceLogicFlow();

                    }

                }



                if (evt.type === 'salesforceUserLogoutEvent') {

                    console.debug('User logout/timeout detected - reloading salesforce script');

                    salesforceLogicFlow();

                }

            });



        });
